The team at A & D are fantastic.  My partner took his Ford Focus (one with all the transmission issues) in and got a motor mount/shaking issue resolved for ~$360, with some other minor services, that the dealership quoted $700.

A week or two afterwards, he noticed his engine overheating and saw that the hose connecting the coolant container to the radiator had a hole worn in it because it was out of its clip and rubbing against an engine belt.  When we took it back to get it taken care of, we mentioned that it could have been a simple mistake of them not putting the hose back after the previous service, since that was the last time anyone was under the hood.

He did an excellent small operation (15mins of surgery) and removed the tumour.  Now my nail is growing back and I've had NO pain since then, and I can sleep well every night, what a relief! After over 10 years, it's magical! Thanks, Dr. Besh!< /Text>

< Review>
TL;DR: Remember the TV show about Dr. House, a physician who loved solving medical mysteries? Well, Dr. Besh is not that kind of doctor. I guess he might be able to help you, if your issue is completely mundane, like a typical case of carpal tunnel syndrome or run-of-the-mill trigger finger. With anything more complicated you'll probably be better off going elsewhere.

I saw Dr. Besh for an injury that was difficult to diagnose. I'd seen another surgeon before him, and that first doctor had told me that he wasn't sure how to treat my injury. Dr. Besh was recommended to me as an experienced hand & wrist specialist, so I decided to get a second opinion from him.

Dr. Besh barely looked at my injury. What he did look at were previous doctor's notes and conclusions from my CT scan and MRI. When I asked why he was only looking at radiologists' conclusions and not at the actual images, he said that according to some study radiologists were better at interpreting them, so he never even tried. Hopefully you can see the problem with his reasoning here.

Dr. Besh essentially took previous physician's notes as gospel. The previous physician wasn't sure what exactly was wrong, and Dr. Besh repeated pretty much the same thing without even trying to perform his own examination.

In an attempt to stimulate his thought process I told him about a case report where a rare injury with symptoms very similar to mine was treated surgically. He looked like I punched him right into his ego. He said that maybe I should see the doctors who wrote that report instead of him. Ironically, that was the only good advice I got from him.

At some point Dr. Besh said "your injury doesn't make sense to me". He speculated that my arm was just stiff from the cast that I wore right after the injury and recommended physical therapy and pain medication. When I asked what pain meds were for, he said that I would need to push through pain when doing PT and therefore would need something to manage pain. Then he stopped and stared at me for several seconds. I guess he was trying to see if I was an addict trying to score some pills. That was quite an unpleasant experience.

I refused the pain meds but decided to give PT a try and talked to a physical therapist working with Dr. Besh. Unlike Dr. Besh he told me that pushing through pain during PT wasn't a good idea, which was more in line with what I'd previously heard from doctors and physical therapists. I asked to show me some exercises and then tried doing those exercises for a few weeks. Apart from increased pain there was absolutely no effect.

Eventually I found a specialist who was able to come up with a more specific diagnosis. It turned out I did need a surgery after all.

Overall I was very disappointed with Dr. Besh. All he did was read me my previous medical records, which I had already read myself and recommended treatment that could cause more harm than good, especially if I did push through pain as he suggested. If I continued working with Dr. Besh, I could still be doing painful and unhelpful physical therapy, possibly getting addicted to opioids in the process.<//Review>

< review>
Ollie had spinal surgery for herniated discs in his lower back a few months ago in Houston. With a lot of after care, he did very well. We moved to California 2 months ago and he continued to recuperate until a few days ago. Same congenital problem. Took him to emergency care at another clinic because Ollie was in pain and began dragging his foot. An anti-inflammatory/pain reliever, sedatives and confinement were prescribed. We could be looking at more surgeries. Took Ollie in to our regular vet at Woodside Vetinary Clinic where they suggested we try an alternative to surgery and another long, painful recovery. Acupuncture. I was apprehensive, but the doctor explained the procedure in great detail and how many dogs find relief (in addition to lifestyle changes).  Very calming and caring staff. Day 1 immediately after acupuncture, Ollie is calm and relaxed.  Also started an anti inflammatory/neuropathic pain reliever, Ollie appears to be pain free and is eating and wagging his tail again. Not so when he was previously sedated and in a zombie state all day. Day 2, still pain free. Will see how it goes after 2 more sessions. Surgery would be the last alternative. Here is Ollie relaxing during his first session. Can barely see the needles. Will update.</review>

<time>1555732111370< /time><rating>5< /rating>< Text>
I have worked with Dr. St. Lawrence and Dr. Calhoun, and have been very impressed with both.

Dr. St. Lawrence was thorough in explaining options for my dog when I brought her in for anxiety and pacing, and happy to answer all of my (many!) questions. He sent follow up emails to check on my dog several weeks after her appointment, and even filled a prescription over email when I decided to get some meds for her a couple months after her anxiety appointment.  I have recommended Woodside to a friend who brought her dog in for blood work, and Dr. St. Lawrence sent her a follow up email to check on her pooch too.

Dr. Calhoun saw my dog for a consultation and then a dental to remove all of her teeth. He was incredibly understanding of my need to understand and know about every charge on our bill, and was very honest about what is and isn't needed and the pros and cons of every decision. On one visit he came out to the waiting room as I was paying just to say goodbye to my dog -- he clearly was enamored with her and it's wonderful to have a vet that so clearly loves pets as much as their owners do. In the weeks after her dental Dr. Calhoun continued to help me figure out the most cost effective plan for post-op pain meds, even if it included ordering some things online not through the clinic.

Do your own research for your needs, but from what I've gathered Woodside seems on the low end cost-wise for vets in this area, and I couldn't be happier with the care my dog has received.

Update: I have since also worked with Dr. Ravn and she was wonderful. SO thoughtful and thorough with explanations and care of my beloved pup.<//Text>

<Text>The Sea View Inn has gotten it right, from the incredible location and views of Manhattan Beach to the down-home charm of vintage art, clean, cozy rooms with lovely views (even from the shower), balconies, and freshly ground coffee, to a heated pool, free use of cruiser bikes and beach gear, convenient parking, and impeccable service. This place has a futuristic-retro vibe that makes us want to return again and again. Meeting the owners was a true pleasure, as I had already been singing their praises to my Girlfriend before I realized who they were. We have both traveled extensively, and highly recommend the Sea View Inn.</Text>< Time>

<Date>1487721600000<//Date><Rate>None< /Rate><text>Our room at the top floor of the northwest unit had a sea view, although not a beach view, so you saw the ocean but not the waves. The two queen beds were very comfortable, the linens and towels were high quality. The room was a good size. The check-in and check-out were easy and the hotel offers free use of bikes and beach equipment (we didnt use those).It was great to have a coffeemaker provided with real coffee rather than the packaged pods. Nice refrigerator and microwave.The location is great for access to local restaurants within 1 to 4 blocks. You could choose from four breakfast spots, pizza, sandwiches, Mexican, beach cuisine, and sports bars, all local rather than chain restaurants.The beach is down a significant hill, but once you take the hike you can enjoy walking or biking on the Strand for miles, wading, surfing, etc.Biggest drawback: The shower has no soap dish at all. You have to put your soap, shower gel, shampoo, etc. on the floor of the shower. Thats a slipping hazard as well as inconvenient. The bathroom itself was quite small without much space to lay out your grooming articles. The shower enclosure goes to the ceiling, I believe, so you cant even bring your own hanging shower trolley to use. This is why I gave room comfort a 3 score.That said, I would likely choose this hotel again as I loved the rest of the features and the location.< /text><Pics>None<//Pics><response>None< /response>< GmapID>

My husband and I stayed here for two nights last April and couldn't have asked for a better place.  Beautiful Manhattan Beach is just a block away and we could see the ocean from our bed.  Our room was lovely, clean, and airy, with a (small) private balcony and sliding glass doors.  We enjoyed shopping and dining on Manhattan Beach Boulevard, a short walk from the inn, and for night there are several local bars just down the street if you don't want to walk that far.  Go get fish and chips at Shellback Tavern while you are there!  If we had more time, we would have loved to borrow bicycles and make use of the convenient paved coastal bike paths.  Highly recommend this place!</Review>

(Translated by Google) Beach Cottage 1 Bedroom - Lower - DO NOT BOOK - JUST A BASEMENT !!!!! Stay from 21/07 to 26/07 - 5 nights
Of our 3 week US tour, this was hands down our worst place to stay. The Sea View Inn website states that this apartment is equipped with a Queen Size bed and a Queen Sofa sleeper. You therefore assume that a family with 2 children can stay perfectly. So nothing true. The apartment is outrageously small! Access to the apartment is via a narrow alley, so you constantly have a view of a blank wall. Just the same on the other side of the apartment, so a view of a blank wall. So absolutely no nice view.
The apartment is hardly suitable for even 2 adults. There are only 2 chairs / bar stools, so certainly not provided for 4 people. Then when you ask for 2 additional seats, they just say they don't have one.
When the seat is converted into a sleeping place, there is no room at all in the "living area". We had to place the coffee table on its narrowest side to make some space.
The bathroom is very small, barely 1 meter wide by approx. 2 meters long (fully enclosed shower, WC and toilet trough included).
The apartment is hardly equipped with a decent closet to place clothes. The bedroom has a built-in wardrobe, but it only has a hanging area. Furthermore, no shelf to put anything on.
On one side of the bed is barely 15 to 20 cm. The same at the foot end. Only on the other side is room with a bedside table and a little space to place the travel suitcases.
The kitchen is completely outdated with hardly any decent facilities to eat something, let alone even prepare something. Refrigerator is many years old and often makes a lot of noise.
When we made our disappointment clear in the reception, the owner appeared to be present. This one minimized the facts and laconically said that we were under no obligation to stay (knowing there was little chance of finding anything else in the high season). About the refrigerator he simply replied that it worked anyway and that we should be satisfied with that. According to the owner, the apartment was presented no differently than it actually is on the website. In our opinion, the photos clearly give a wider view than reality.
The owner was just the first unfriendly American we meet on our vacation. He himself said that we just shouldn't be so rude and aggressive.
Based on the many reviews, the other apartments will in all probability meet today's standards, but the apartment where we stayed certainly does not. Outrageously expensive for what we got for our money.
As for the accommodations that are provided, the bicycles may be better maintained. Not a single bike that was in good order.
Only plus for us was the location. The apartment and the entire complex of Sea View Inn is located 250 meters from the beach. Hence the only star we give.
We will never come back here !!!!

(Original)
Beach Cottage 1 Bedroom - Lower - NIET BOEKEN - PRECIES EEN KELDER !!!!! Verblijf van 21/07 tot 26/07 - 5 nachten
Van onze 3 weekse rondreis in de VS was dit zonder meer onze slechtste verblijfplaats.  Op de website van Sea View Inn staat vermeld dat dit appartement voorzien is van een Queen Size bed en een Queen Sofa sleeper.  Je gaat er dus vanuit dat er perfect kan verbleven worden door een gezin met 2 kinderen.  Niets van waar dus.  Het appartement is schandalig klein!  Toegang tot het appartement is via een smal steegje waardoor je dus voortdurend uitkijkt op een blinde muur.  Aan de andere kant van het appartement net hetzelfde, zicht op een blinde muur dus.  Dus absoluut geen enkel mooi uitzicht.
Het appartement is zelfs nauwelijks geschikt voor 2 volwassenen.  Er zijn slechts 2 stoelen/barkrukken, dus zeker niet voorzien voor 4 personen.  Als je dan 2 bijkomende stoelen gaat vragen, dan zeggen ze gewoon dat ze er geen hebben.
Wanneer de zetel wordt omgevormd naar slaapplaats is er helemaal geen plaats meer in het "leefgedeelte". De salontafel dienden we op zijn smalste kant te plaatsen om toch wat ruimte te maken.
De badkamer is bijzonder klein, nauwelijks 1 meter breed op ca. 2 meter lang (volledig ingesloten douche, WC en toilettafal inbegrepen).
Het appartement is nauwelijks voorzien van een deftige kast om kleding te plaatsen.  In de slaapkamer is wel een ingebouwde kast maar deze is enkel voorzien van een hanggedeelte.  Verder geen enkele legplank om iets op te leggen.
Aan de ene kant van het bed is amper 15 √† 20 cm.  Hetzelfde aan het voeteinde.  Enkel aan de andere kant is ruimte waar een nachtkastje staat en daarnaast nog een beetje plaats om de reiskoffers te plaatsen.
De keuken is totaal verouderd met nauwelijks deftige voorzieningen om iets te eten, laat staan zelfs iets te bereiden.  Koelkast is vele jaren oud en maakt regelmatig een hels lawaai.
Wanneer we in de receptie onze ontgoocheling duidelijk maakten, bleek de eigenaar aanwezig te zijn.  Deze minimaliseerde de feiten en zei lakoniek dat we niet verplicht waren om te blijven (wetende dat er in het hoogseizoen weinig kans was om iets anders te vinden).  Over de koelkast antwoordde hij gewoon dat ze toch werkte en dat we daarmee tevreden dienden te zijn.  Volgens eigenaar werd op de website het appartement niet anders voorgesteld dan deze in werkelijkheid is.  Volgens onze mening geven de foto's duidelijk een ruimere weergave dan de realiteit.
De eigenaar was gewoon de eerste onvriendelijke Amerikaan die we ontmoeten tijdens onze vakantie. Zelf zei hij dat we gewoon niet zo onbeleefd en agressief diende te zijn.
Afgaand op de vele recencies zullen de andere appartementen naar alle waarschijnlijkheid wel voldoen aan de normen van vandaag, maar het appartement waar wij verbleven doet dit zeker niet.  Schandalig duur voor wat we kregen voor ons geld.
Wat betreft de accomodaties die geleverd worden, mogen de fietsen beter onderhouden worden.  Geen enkele fiets die deftig in orde was.
Enig pluspunt voor ons was de locatie.  Het appartement en het volledige complex van Sea View Inn is gelegen op een 250-tal meter van het strand.  Vandaar ook de enige ster die wij geven.
Hier komen wij nooit terug!!!!<//text>

<user_name>Marisela C< /user_name><Time>1566143021427</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
My girlfriend and I went there for our 1 year anniversary because we wanted to splurge a little. Side note: And also because we're boycotting Olive Garden for supporting Trump's reelection.

First, the service was great. All of the servers were aware of our needs and were filling up our waters almost every time they walked by. Second, the dinner was absolutely DELICIOUS and SIMPLE.

My girlfriend got the gnocchi al pesto and the pesto, you can tell, is homemade and absolutely delicious with blasts of flavor. Plus the gnocchi was incredibly soft, it complemented everything so well. I received the penne with the vodka sauce without bacon because we're vegetarian and OH MY WORD, that pasta dish was made with so much jam packed flavor. The sauce was absolutely amazing. Overall these two dishes tasted incredibly authentic and the portions were absolutely perfect and worth the price.

The dessert was probably the biggest surprise of the night. We opted out for the almond chocolate cake and salted caramel gelato with raspberry sauce. WOW. That's all I have to say.

You can truly tell this restaurant cares about being authentic and utilizing fresh ingredients that have incredible flavor. Will definitely be coming back for another special occasion and I highly recommend supporting this local place if you live in the Downtown San Jose area. Thank you for having us and being LGBTQ+ friendly!</Review>

< user>
110201923536480543982< /user>
< Name>
Bruce MacNaughton</Name>
< time>
1548168359460<//time>
<rate>5</rate>< Text>
Excellent Italian food served by slightly harried waiters in a comfortable setting. We both chose appetizers and an entree.

My wife had a seafood sampler from the regular menu - it was exceptional with squid, tuna, scallops, and shrimp. There was a light sauce that enhanced, not overpowered, the seafood. I chose the Jota alla Triestina (borlotti bean soup) from their Friuli menu and it was an exceptional rustic soup, hearty but not rich.

We both ordered entrees from the Friuli menu. The Risotto Miramare was excellent with perfect risotto and seafood (shrimp, calamari, crab) in every bite. Balanced with peas and tomatoes it was a fantastic meal. The Gamberoni alla Busara was amazing - prawns larger than some lobster tails sauteed in paprika, garlic, brandy, capers, marinara and cream.

After our food we didn't have dessert because we were full. But I'm excited to check back for their regional specialties coming up.<//Text>

< review>
solid and dependable.  it‚Äôs a chain so you can basically go anywhere and get the same consistency.  plus it has been around for a long time so there‚Äôs that.

service was slow on the saturday before christmas but to be expected.  no real issues there but just be advised.

location is in the westin san jose downtown (formerly the saint claire).  parking in the area kinda sucks.  street meters max out at an hour and there is public lot across the street but at $6/hour and a $22 max it‚Äôs really not a bargain.  valet at the hotel is $15 for the first two hours with validation or $30 after that.  so factor that in.  dinging a star because of this.

food was solid if not remarkable.  parents had the tagliatelle and the linguine mare and i had the ravioli.  it‚Äôs tasty but not amazing (sorry, i got spoiled living in NYC for nine years).

worth a visit if in downtown SJ, mostly because italian here in general is very meh.  this is better than most and the decor is great.</review>

< text>
We stopped in here before a show downtown. The ambiance was ok, it was around 6pm and the afternoon sun was blazing thru the windows making it pretty warm in there. I had the Tagletell bolognese and my husband had the veal. Both were good sized portions. My pasta was great. It was toothsome and perfectly al dente. The bolognese sauce was quite tasty. My husband's veal however, not so good. The sauce was lemony and bright but the veal was tough and the thin coating of flour that should have been crispy was kinda gummy. The vegetable side was a giant broccoli stem and carrot that were undercooked. The food came out fast, which was nice since we were eating pre- show, but we had to ask several times for bread (it finally came to our table after our food arrived), and our waters were never refilled. The place was fairly busy but it was a Wednesday evening at 6pm. Overall I would say this place is ok if you get pasta, but they really need to improve their service.</text>

<user_id>110889359600338463075<//user_id>< Name>
Merry Yen< /Name>
< time>
1427654240708<//time>
<rate>2</rate>< text>
We had dinner at Il Fornaio on Friday evening and it was a disappointing dining experience.
The restaurant wasn't very busy when we arrived, but it took the front door a while to seat us.   It then took our server a while to take our drink order, and by then we were ready to order our entrees.
Bread came warm to the table, which was one of the highlights of the meal.  My cannellini bean soup was the other highlight - rich, hearty, and flavorful.
3 out of the 4 entrees were less than expected - the meat in my bolognese sauce was very dry.  My friend got the grilled salmon (on the specials menu) and it was overcooked.  The spinach that came with it looked like it was previously frozen - it was gray and wilted.  My husband got the rigatoni with the vodka cream sauce and it was just meh.  The dishes lacked presentation and flavor, and several items were overcooked.
Service was cordial but on the slower side.
I don't think we'll return to Il Fornaio any time soon.<//text>
